Current Affairs Commentary

The Problem of Controlled Economy 17

— Cun

Recently, the Shanghai yarn industry, due to the Cotton Industry Control Committee's move to stabilize yarn prices, ordered the exchange to refuse new cotton yarn delivered by customer manufacturers from November to December of this year. This caused a huge uproar. Afterwards, the Cotton Industry Control Committee announced the process of handling this matter on the 12th of this month. In our observation, this is actually a matter that cannot be ignored in the process of implementing controlled economy after the establishment of the National Economic Commission.

Advanced capitalist countries today, such as Germany, Italy, Britain and the United States, have all adopted a policy of actively intervening in national economic facilities in recent years. This is where the slogan of controlled economy chanted by European and American countries after the occurrence of the economic panic comes from. And its goal is nothing more than to raise or stabilize prices in order to restore social prosperity. In terms of its methods, there are thousands of strands, and the meticulous calculations are all based on suitability for the country as a prerequisite. It is impossible to imitate arbitrarily and expect unexpected gains, and the reasons for the occurrence of their panic seem to have other real reasons at the root. This one problem alone cannot save it.

If we talk about the future of the so-called controlled economy plan in light of our country's current national conditions, it is not easy to be optimistic. First, the government's financial resources are exhausted. At present, the central government's income and expenditure are not small, reaching about 200 million a year. The government's own expenses are not easy to maintain. Where does the surplus power come from to save today's panic? Seeking to spend money like the governments of European and American countries to equalize prices and manipulate exchange rates, which exceeds hundreds of millions, is certainly not something that can be said in today's China. Second, the weakness of our country's financial efforts is also undeniable. The current status of the financial industry is not only hindered by the continuous economic depression of industry and commerce, but also unable to seek self-rescue due to the concentration of financial resources of foreign banks. If the authorities only advocate the movement of controlled economy, without a strong financial organization to dominate the operation of the national economy, the result may be nothing more than wasting expenses. Third, the dumping of foreign goods is also a major obstacle. In recent years, the spread of domestic depression is due to the increasingly narrow sales of important commodities, which leads to overproduction in the country. The reasons for causing overproduction, such as the loss of markets in the Northeast, the bankruptcy of rural villages in the interior, and the development of foreign factories, are all obvious facts. And especially the increase in foreign goods is not to be underestimated. If the authorities really want to seek price stability and economic control, they must first make the production of foreign factories and the import of foreign goods subject to appropriate regulation, otherwise the so-called control will only benefit other countries, and it will be of no benefit to our industry, commerce, or the people.

Therefore, what we hope for from the government today is that in order to carry out a controlled economy and realize price stability, it must establish a comprehensive plan that cannot be limited to the issue of collecting several tens of thousands of bags of yarn. It should focus on the various reasons for the decline in yarn prices and try to find fundamental solutions.

With Firm and Euphemistic Wording, France Replies to Hitler: It Will Never Abandon the League of Nations and Disarmament; It Is Ready to Open Negotiations with Germany at Any Time; It Is Difficult to Agree to Equality Without Guaranteed Security 18

(Paris) Tonight, after the Chamber of Deputies debated foreign policy, it passed a vote of confidence in the Sarraut government by a large majority, with 395 votes in favor and 154 votes against. The motion called on the government's policy to be loyal to the League of Nations, to expand France's friendship, to act for international unity, and to be vigilant in seeking equality and security for all nations, and to realize fair disarmament. The left wing and the left-center party voted in favor of the government, while the right wing and the right-center party voted against. In his speech at the end of the debate, Premier Sarraut said that the government's reply to Hitler could be summed up in one sentence: fearless. But at the same time, it contained the desire to save peace through Geneva and to reach an understanding with Germany. Sarraut advised France, which has material and military strength, to rise up to prevent any narrow-minded dictators and to remain calm. He continued that if France wants to continue to conclude peace and security agreements, France must make concessions. Although less than yesterday, he is willing to announce to the world that France will never abandon Geneva and will never abandon the League of Nations Disarmament Conference. Sarraut also solemnly declared that the Chamber of Deputies unanimously opposed the "war-stopping settlement" and knew that the alliance system could not succeed because it was too weak. In response to Hitler's expression of his desire for peace and understanding, Sarraut said that France also shared this desire, but France and the countries that signed the agreement on Germany's request for equality and reciprocity would say "No" to them as long as the security issue was set aside for a long time. Sarraut added that France is ready to talk to Germany, but it must be done through normal channels and in the light of international agreements. (14th Reuters Telegram)

Declaration by the Jiang Government: With Strong National Power, There Is Nothing to Fear; Ready for Peaceful Accommodation with Germany 19

(Paris) As mentioned in the previous telegram, the Chamber of Deputies voted in favor of the government's motion yesterday. Before the vote, Premier Sarraut took the stage to give a speech, saying that the relationship between France and Germany is a matter of peace. Some people have heard that after the German referendum, what does the French government intend to do? We answered that what the government should do is first to remain calm and not to disturb anyone, so as to calmly wait for the development of the situation. This is extremely easy, because France has 40 million people, and its material and military strength are sufficient to defend itself without fear of others adding violence. France's desire for peace has been consistent from beginning to end, and has not changed at all at present. The result of the German referendum only makes France's aspirations more determined. France will not retreat on anything that should not be conceded.

Seeking to Maintain Unity with Various Nations 20

The League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference have always been France's shield. The attitude of France's allies and the United Nations may waver. We must strive to maintain a unified stance. These countries each have their concerns, and we must understand them, not hastily blame them. However, for their benefit, they should unite with France and maintain European peace with a frank attitude, even where global peace is threatened. This is what all allies and the United Nations should understand. (Applause in the chamber.) The brewing disaster can only be avoided by all nations reaching a proper agreement. France's policies can gain the support of most countries in the world. France's national strength is sufficiently robust to protect its legitimate rights. As for armaments, there must be solid guarantees before France will agree to reductions. Sarraut continued, viewing the progress of the Disarmament Conference, if a disarmament convention is to be established and Germany is to participate (if Germany truly desires to maintain peace), it should be based on the points already agreed upon by the United Kingdom, the United States, France, and Italy. Sarraut reiterated Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour's declaration, saying that the government will never disregard any proposals beneficial to peace. Then, he addressed the German people, saying:

French Prime Minister's Message to the German People 21

You say you aspire to peace, but are the hopes of the French people any different? The spirit of Briand's policies lies entirely in this. We hold the same thoughts towards Germany. We absolutely do not wish for the decline of Germany. Germany, a nation of sixty million people, to wish for its demise, ask yourselves, could the French people entertain such a delusion? France genuinely desires Germany to enjoy its rightful rights. France is not insensitive to Germany's suffering. France will not hinder Germany's economic development. Therefore, France at all times and in all places wants to approach France and reach a compromise.

After this explanation, we have the right to declare that France should, based on this spirit of compromise, seek to resolve the issue of equal rights to armaments. Germany, based on the declaration of the United Kingdom, France, and Italy on December 11 of the seventh year, demands equal rights to armaments. It must be understood that equality of armaments must be exchanged for security to be implemented. These two things are closely related and indispensable. However, Germany only demands equality of armaments and disregards security. This is not something France can accept. Such one-sided equality of armaments will not only be rejected by France but also probably not recognized by the countries that signed the declaration of December 11 last year.

Despite this, France is still prepared to negotiate, but with two conditions: (1) The talks must be conducted in the full view of the international community and must respect countries with special ties to France. (2) What exactly is to be negotiated? France should know this beforehand. What is the basis for the negotiations that Germany wants to conduct? This must be clearly stated. After these two conditions are met, France will return to Geneva to continue working on the construction of peace. Whether Germany participates or not is acceptable. In this way, France can once again show the world the righteousness of its intentions. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

European Peace Depends on Franco-German Relations: Paul-Boncour Announces Policy Towards Germany 22

(Paris) French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour, with resolute but moderate words, responded to German Chancellor Hitler's speech on Sunday, saying that France has no other course of action except to abide by the conventions concluded by the League of Nations in broad daylight. France is prepared to negotiate at any time, but any agreement between France and Germany must be concluded in Geneva. The order and security of Europe are now in danger due to Germany's fanatical nationalism. The neighboring countries of Germany are expressing anxiety, and not without reason. If Germany re-arms, then France must also add armaments, and the result will be extremely fierce competition. But each country has ambassadors stationed. If France receives any concrete proposals from Germany, France is willing to consider them in the spirit that it has always treated this great nation, because it knows that the peace of Europe largely depends on relations with Germany. Paul-Boncour spoke at length on the international situation and continued, saying that France's responsibility is to protect the French in the Saar region. The joint responsibility of the French government and the League of Nations is to monitor the Saar plebiscite held in 1935 to ensure that it is based on genuine popular will. (Reuters dispatch on the 14th)

(Berlin) The Cabinet has appointed General von Papen as Germany's Saar Commissioner to handle various issues related to the territory. (Reuters dispatch on the 14th)

Germany's Demands Will Become More Urgent; France Pays Diplomatic Attention 23

(Paris) A major debate on foreign policy was held in the Chamber of Deputies this afternoon. As a result of the final vote, the Chamber expressed its confidence in the government by a majority of 395 votes to 194. The details of the debate are recorded below. The Chamber of Deputies convened at 3:10 p.m. The number of attendees was high. Initially, the number of parliamentarians who attended was small, but the seat filled up quickly. Prime Minister Sarraut, Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour, and cabinet members entered the hall one after another, and sat in government seats. Then, Socialist Party Member Nogaro spoke first, followed by a speech by Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour, who said that Hitler's revolution in Germany had been recognized by the people in last week's vote. Germany's demands will become more urgent. Although the speeches of various important figures in the German authorities have repeatedly stated their desire for peace, the principles of victory in Germany contain various dangers. Neighboring countries of Germany cannot but pay attention to it diplomatically. Although Germany has withdrawn from the League of Nations, it has never changed its policy towards nations who are sympathetic to Geneva. France advocates continuing disarmament work and striving for the establishment of a disarmament convention, and has always believed that it is appropriate to unite all countries so that a disarmament convention can be concluded. We are unwilling to bear any responsibility for Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference.

Locarno Treaty Provides Guarantees for Germany 24

However, since the principles of offensive and defensive alliances between countries before the European War have been prohibited by the League of Nations, we can only try to develop new treaties concluded within the League of Nations. For example, the Locarno Treaty is still completely intact. This treaty is still a guarantee treaty for our country, and the same is true for Germany. Its value is equal to the treaty that guaranteed Belgium's neutrality before the European War. The reason why the United Kingdom participated in the war with all its strength was to fulfill such treaties.

Four-Power Pact Improves Franco-Italian Relations 25

The conclusion of the Four-Power Pact eliminated misunderstandings between us and Italy. This treaty is implemented in accordance with the principles of the League of Nations. The reason why this treaty does not hinder the relationship between France and the Little Entente countries and Poland is precisely because of this. Moreover, the French government is not only willing to overturn its current diplomatic policy but also wants to promote diplomatic relations and compromises with foreign countries. France's new friendships are increasing day by day, but old friendships remain unchanged.

Germany is Welcome to Negotiate at Any Time 26

As for Germany, if it wants to change its mind and is willing to cooperate with countries that are determined to maintain peace, Germany is free to do so. The key lies entirely in Germany itself. France adopts a "be there any time" policy for diplomatic negotiations, but if there is a compromise, it must first consult with countries that will clearly conclude a treaty with France within the scope of the League of Nations before proceeding. We will implement all these policies with all our strength and enthusiasm. Please judge whether it is appropriate.

France's Population is Less Than Germany's 27

After Paul-Boncour finished speaking, Fabry, a member of the Republican Center Party, said that Germany's arms manufacturing capacity is superior to France's, and France's population is smaller than Germany's. (According to the report, France's population is 40 million, and Germany's is 65 million.) France's borders are vulnerable to attack in many places. Equality of armaments is actually disadvantageous to France. Therefore, France hopes that the government will not reduce its armaments. Socialist Party member Nenjay and former Prime Minister Tardieu spoke briefly one after another. Finally, Puy-Homme, a member who does not represent any political party, delivered a speech, launching a fierce attack on the Sarraut government, and said that the Treaty of Versailles prohibited military training outside of the army, but the governments of various countries failed to effectively implement the treaty, causing Germany to violate it. Puy-Homme also attacked the Four-Power Pact, and said that the trial period for the arms inspection system was opposed by the United Kingdom. Minister of the Army Ladreit de Lacharrière then presented and read out the record of the Anglo-French talks on September 23, which clearly stated that British Foreign Secretary Simon unconditionally agreed to the four-year arms inspection trial period and the dissolution of military groups outside the German regular army. When the Chamber of Deputies continued to meet in the evening, Prime Minister Sarraut said that France's spiritual, material, and military strength are sufficient to continue to engage in international cooperation. Then, a vote was taken to express confidence in the government's proposal, which was passed by a majority of 395 votes to 194. (Havas dispatch on the 14th)

Mussolini Expresses the Way for Europe to Save Itself: The League of Nations Has Lost Its Meaning; All Nations Must Seek Compromise 28

Rome. Today, Prime Minister Mussolini gave a speech at the National Council of Corporations, first stating that "the existence of capitalism has experienced a crisis." Mussolini believed that capitalism, in order to maintain itself, wants to maintain continuous consumption. Unexpectedly, supply exceeds demand, so production cannot be sold. Capitalism is turning to the state for help. The crisis in Europe is not only a panic for capitalism, but also involves political and cultural issues. Those who control the world are no longer the European continent. West of the Atlantic, a new continent has risen to compete for hegemony. Japan in the Far East has also made great progress. Japanese silk fabrics have been sold in Italian markets. The Prime Minister then stated that the National Council of Corporations is specifically a kind of political organization and conference, and what it is committed to will be the issue of the European political crisis. The Prime Minister said, "Europe can still save itself, but there must be a minimum degree of compromise among all nations, and it must be effective. However, the League of Nations has now lost its meaning. The various principles of the League of Nations are all good, but it has no power to implement them. As for the Four-Power Pact, although no one praises it, it has never been forgotten in everyone's mind."

Corporatist System Replaces Parliament 29

In the second part of his speech, the Prime Minister explained the organization of Italian corporations, briefly saying, "Even if Italy has the possibility of implementing capitalism, it is unwilling to do so. Italy should be a country with a mixed economy, and focus on agriculture." The Prime Minister then declared that the Chamber of Deputies will be dissolved after its current term expires. This kind of parliament is an organ for enemy parties to govern, and is fundamentally opposed to pan-nationalism. After its abolition, it will be replaced by the National Council of Corporations. Mussolini concluded that "we are now abolishing economic liberalism and adopting a corporatist policy. In other words, it is controlling the economy. Socialism and economic liberalism grew up at the same time, declined at the same time, and corporatism will rise to replace them. The world economic panic has reached this point, and corporatism will inevitably be adopted by the world." (Havas dispatch on the 14th)

Japan's Westward Advance is a Political Issue 30

"Rome" Prime Minister Mussolini's speech at the National Council of Corporations has been seen in the previous telegram. The following is an excerpt from the speech, which originally stated that "Japan in the Far East, after its contact with Europe through the Russo-Japanese War in 1905, has taken steps to advance westward. This is actually a political issue. The reason why we regard it as a political issue is because Japan's contact with Europe is actually of a political nature. Today, if Europe can find the minimum level of political organization, then Europe can still try to regain the helm of the world's culture. What we relied on in the past as a permanent standard should still be followed today, but to achieve the realization of European political understanding, we must correct the injustices of the past, because a kind of injustice has now created an extremely serious situation." Belgian Senator Publishes Secret Documents: Germany Has Not Fulfilled the Peace Treaty and Disarmed 31

Brussels Belgian Senator Allart made a statement to the committees of the two houses of parliament, saying that he had obtained the report of the Inter-Allied Military Control Commission, which was made by British General Morgan in 1927. The report was obtained from the Allied side, and only the governments of the Allied countries have a copy, which has not been published. Its contents prove that Germany has not disarmed in accordance with the Treaty of Versailles. The last chapter of the report was published in "La Nation Belge" this morning. The title of the last chapter of 比利時民族 is "Summary and Conclusions." The content summarizes the facts obtained from the investigation and various reservations, stating that the inspection is limited to the externally visible stored weapons, so the inspection results can only obtain relative truth. Germany has a large amount of weapons stored, and many hidden military materials. The annual military budget has increased. Despite repeated protests from the Inspection Commission and repeated warnings from the Allied governments, they were ignored. The actual amount used for armaments is very large, and cannot be concealed even by disguising it as normal expenses. The clauses in the peace treaty regarding the construction of barracks and other military buildings have not been implemented. The regulations of the People's National Defence Forces, which are formulated in accordance with the troop levels, weapons, and military needs of large countries, have not been modified in accordance with the provisions of the peace treaty. The report concludes that, under the current circumstances, no one can automatically declare that Germany has at least implemented the military clauses of the Treaty of Versailles in spirit. It must be until the various corrections that the report indicates as necessary have made great progress, and until it can finally be considered to have reached the disarmament stage expected by the Treaty of Versailles, before this is possible. But now Germany is still very far from this stage. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

Critical Situation in British-Irish Relations: Ireland to Declare Republic; United Kingdom Indicates Difficult Recognition 34

(London) Today in the House of Commons, British Secretary of State for Dominion Affairs Thomas claimed that three bills currently proposed by the Irish Free State parliament seek to amend the constitution and, in the view of the British government, are related to the revocation of the Anglo-Irish Treaty. This bill seeks to transfer the power of the British representative to propose appropriation funds to the Executive Council, abolish the British representative's right to veto bills, and abolish the right to appeal to the Privy Council. From the meaning of this case, it can also be seen that South Ireland clearly intends to gradually delete the royal power from the constitution. The purpose of Eamon de Valera, President of the South Irish government, is to create a united Irish Republic under the British Empire. This kind of approach is absolutely not to be recognized. According to the declaration of the 1926 Imperial Conference, the relationship between the United Kingdom and the self-governing territories under the Crown must recognize that the Irish Free State, according to its legal status, is not within the scope of the Empire. Since the Free State is completely free to self-govern its internal affairs, other parts of the Empire are given great convenience. The Free State is now losing the benefits of being ordinary citizens and the economic preferences in trade with other parts of the Empire through its own actions, and will lose the opportunity to exercise its power in international affairs. All these privileges and responsibilities coexist. What are the responsibilities? Namely, to respect royal power, faithfully abide by contracts, and express friendship and cooperation with other parts of the Empire. The British government wants to see the Free State occupy a complete position in the British Empire, accept its responsibilities, and enjoy its privileges. But if the Free State abandons its responsibilities, it cannot hope to enjoy privileges. (Reuters dispatch on the 14th)

(London) South Ireland's intention to delete royal power from the constitution is now making the situation between Britain and Ireland increasingly critical. If the Free State insists on its own way, serious consequences will inevitably occur. President of the Free State de Valera told a Reuters reporter in Dublin that his answer to the remarks of British Secretary of State for Dominion Affairs Thomas was clearly decided by the Irish people in 1918. Those who agreed to the 1921 treaty abandoned the republic in order to avoid the terrible war threatened by then British Prime Minister George. The British government has always claimed that if the Irish people exercise their basic right to choose their own constitution, Britain will regard it as an act of hostility and take it as a reason for aggression. If the British government declares tomorrow that the declaration of a republic is not a reason for an aggressive hostile act, then this matter can be resolved. (Reuters dispatch on the 15th)

International Silk Congress Opens; Discussions on Japanese Goods and Competition in the World Market 36

(Paris) The International Silk Congress opened here today. It is currently discussing the competition of Japanese goods in the world silk market. The discussion is centered on the proposals put forward by the London Silk Association, the Lyon Silk Manufacturers Association, and the Swiss Silk Manufacturers Association, which call for revising the ratio of Japanese natural silk and artificial silk fabric imports. Speakers all said that it is impossible to compete in the open market with the products of countries with low living costs and labor conditions that cannot be compared with those of Europe and the United States. The proposal stated that the ratio is based on the average number of silk exports from Japan from 192 to 1931. Representatives from the United Kingdom, France, Italy, and Switzerland attended the congress. (National Telegram on the 14th)

Anglo-American-Japanese Naval Competition: United Kingdom Unwilling to Be Weaker Than United States and Japan; Decides to Build Three Large Cruisers 37

(London) After careful consideration of the cruiser programs of countries such as Japan and the United States, the British Admiralty has decided to revise the 1933 program, including two new cruisers of approximately nine thousand tons and improved armaments, and one Arethusa-class cruiser of five thousand two hundred tons. This news was announced today in the House of Commons by Secretary of the Admiralty Monsell. Monsell claimed that the government's previous decision to build cruisers of smaller tonnage was in the hope that other countries would do the same. In July last year, the British representative in Geneva proposed reducing future cruisers to seven thousand tons, with a maximum cannon bore of six o'clock. It was also hoped that this proposal would be accepted by all countries. Unfortunately, neither of the above two hopes was realized. In 1931, Japan built two cruisers of eight thousand five hundred tons each, armed with fifteen six-inch guns. The British government has now heard that Japan is building two cruisers of the same tonnage again, and plans to add two more, for a total of six. The United States has also stated that it plans to build four ten thousand ton cruisers, each carrying fifteen six-inch guns. If the previously approved British program is implemented, the new British cruisers will be far inferior to other countries. (According to the report, the original British program included one 7250-ton cruiser with 8-inch guns and three 5400-ton cruisers with 6-inch guns.) The total tonnage of British cruisers is limited by the London Naval Treaty, putting it in a dilemma. If the original program is followed, the ships built will be inferior to certain cruisers built by other countries. If cruisers comparable to other countries are built, the four ships must be reduced to three. The Admiralty has repeatedly considered that it is better to have fewer ships than to have ships that are inferior in strength to other countries. Therefore, it has decided to propose revising the 1933 program. This revision will increase the cost of the 1933 program and is expected to slightly reduce the number of cruisers that Japan and the United States can build in accordance with the London Naval Treaty. However, the British government's policy will continue to strive to limit the larger number of ships and the maximum tonnage per ship by common agreement. (Reuters dispatch on the 14th)

(Moscow) Stalin's report on the achievements of the Five-Year Plan to the Central Executive Committee of the Communist Party in January this year has now been translated into Chinese by the Moscow Foreign Workers Publishing House and printed in five thousand copies. (National Telegram on the 14th)

(London) The Admiralty's decision to build larger cruisers to prevent naval powers from exceeding the strength of the United Kingdom is reviewed by various parties who believe that naval competition has already begun. Soviet Russian Defense; Left Bank of the Heilongjiang River Covered in Barbed Wire; Many Fortresses Turn Riverbank into Fortress 43

A Harbin dispatch from the North China Daily News on the 5th states that Japanese Major General Tashiro recently flew from Qiqihar to Sakhalin Island and back to inspect the situation on both banks of the Heilongjiang River. According to his report after returning to Qiqihar, Soviet Russian military preparations far exceeded his expectations. For example, the left bank of the Heilongjiang River, opposite the Manchurian border, is covered with barbed wire for several miles, so that no one can cross into Russian territory after the river freezes. Along the river, strong fortresses are set up at intervals, either built with cement or just earthen fortifications, turning the riverbank into a line of fortresses. Only the Soviet Russian side of the river has frozen, and it is expected that the entire river will freeze within a week. Within two weeks, the army can cross over the ice. Soviet Russia has clearly prepared for this unexpected danger, without a doubt. Recently, the railway bureau authorities have been very frugal, resulting in the Chinese Eastern Railway having only enough coal for eight days. Due to the shortage of coal, some trains have been ordered to burn firewood, so that regular passenger and freight trains will not have a coal shortage. The Mutanjiang coal mine is difficult to protect from bandits, but is still operating as usual. The Zhalainuo'er coal mine is also operating as usual, but shipments from the south seem to have decreased. It is said that this is due to the frequent transportation of Japanese troops and supplies, resulting in insufficient freight cars. In the past three weeks, White Russians in Harbin have been moving south to find work in various parts of China, especially Shanghai. However, some are now returning, claiming that there is nothing to be found in Shanghai, and it is better to return to Harbin.

Principles of the Stamp Tax Law 45

(Nanjing) The principles of the Stamp Tax Law passed by the Central Political Council on the 15th are recorded below: (1) Stamp tax shall be levied on certificates concerning the creation, alteration, transfer, inheritance, and proof of property rights in civil or commercial matters, but those not intended to take effect or without business or obligation are exempt. (2) Stamp tax shall be levied on documents submitted to public agencies or presented to schools by individuals or organizations for requests or statements, and on notarized documents issued by public agencies or schools due to individual or organizational relations, but those issued for the collection of donations or already affixed with judicial stamps are exempt. (3) As a principle, government-run businesses shall pay stamp tax. (4) In order to encourage savings, support agriculture and industry, and facilitate travel, the certificates and books used for savings undertakings (excluding prize savings), agriculture and industry, and travel shall be reduced or exempted as appropriate. (5) Those with greater validity or rights, or with longer use periods, shall be taxed heavily, and those with lighter validity or rights, or with shorter use periods, shall be taxed lightly. (6) Certificates of common behavior mostly adopt simple and easy fixed-amount tax, and certificates of rare behavior mostly adopt easy-to-calculate progressive tax. (7) The types and names of certificates adopt a generalized approach, but still focus on their nature as a standard for taxation, and those with different natures shall not be compared. (8) It is specified who should be responsible for paying taxes for which certificates. (9) The difference between the minimum and maximum amount of fines should not be too long, and the amount of fines should be determined according to the amount of tax evasion. (10) When discovering evidence of multiple tax evasions by the same party, all should be combined and not punished on a case-by-case basis. (11) The procedures for sentencing and executing fines should be specified in detail. (Central News Agency, 14th)

Postal Workers' Union Proposes Conditions in the Case of the Conflict Between the Police and Postal Workers on the Nanjing Railway 52

(Nanjing) The Nanjing Postal Workers' Union has stated that the incident of the conflict between the police and postal workers on the railway has not yet been resolved. The union sent a letter to the Jiangsu-Anhui Postal Administration, proposing seven conditions: (1) The railway police should be fully responsible if there is any blame for the delay of 39 bags and 11 sets of Wujiang mail that day, which included many mails sent to the bandit-controlled areas. (2) The new railway station building was originally intended to facilitate the transportation of mail for passengers. It should facilitate the transportation of mail and assist in the quick delivery of mail. In the future, the location for parking cars and the postal workers' transportation of mail should still be designated at the south entrance of Rehe Road. (3) Punish the violent railway police. (4) The railway bureau should be responsible for the medical expenses and substitute labor costs of the injured postal workers. (5) If there are any changes in the route for the transportation of mail on the platform in the future, please notify the post office in writing in advance, otherwise all disputes will be the responsibility of the railway bureau. (6) Whenever postal workers are working at the station, even if they do not follow instructions, they should be notified at any time. The receiving clerk shall not arbitrarily arrest the postal workers, so as not to delay official business and violate laws and regulations. (7) Guarantee that the incident of arbitrarily arresting and injuring postal workers will not happen again. (Special Dispatch, 15th)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Communications approved a letter from the Hong Kong Post Office, stating that the electrical transmission of our country's coastal radio stations during International Quiet Time is a violation of international conventions. Continued Payment of Interest on the Road Redemption Loan 64

(Nanjing) The principal and interest on the Daokou-Qinghua Railway's road redemption loan to the Fu Corporation have not been repaid since 1926. The British merchants have repeatedly urged payment. A certain amount has now been accumulated. The Ministry of Railways and the Fu Corporation have been notified to begin continuing to pay the interest on the road redemption loan for the first half of 1926. Among them, the Fu Joint Office has accumulated arrears of freight totaling over 216,700 yuan as of the end of October, and the Zhongyuan Company has newly accumulated freight arrears of over 93,100 yuan, totaling over 300,000 yuan, which are currently being urged. Branch bureaus will be set up in Shantou and areas along the Northeast River where tungsten is abundant. According to the government, tungsten is crucial for national revenue and defense. The 37th Army Corps Commits Large-Scale Plundering in Xuwang; National Army Feigns Retreat to Lure Bandits, Fierce Battle for Two Days and Nights; 3,000 Bandits Killed, Over 800 Guns Seized; Will Now Focus on Eliminating the Pseudo-1st Army Corps;剿 Bandit Mission Soon to Achieve Complete Success 75

Nanchang Dispatch: Since the beginning of the month, the pseudo-Front Army in the eastern border area of Zixi, Lichuan, Nancheng, and Nanfeng has repeatedly sent small groups of bandits to harass the positions of the National Army, intending to probe the National Army's strength and weaknesses, and then concentrate on attacking a single point. Therefore, the bandits' tracks are extremely elusive, but the National Army is waiting for them and the bandits cannot succeed. Finally, on the 10th of this month, with the pseudo-15th Army Corps in the rear and the pseudo-37th Army Corps in front, they began to advance westward, hiding during the day and moving at night, rushing into Jinxi. Commander-in-Chief Jiang and Commander Gu clearly saw through the bandits' schemes, so they ordered the troops stationed in various streams and locations in Lichuan to pretend not to resist and allow them to pass through the defensive positions. At the same time, they ordered a certain unit in Jinxi to falsely retreat towards the Linchuan border. The Red bandits did not realize this and went deep, vainly attempting to directly attack the rear of Fuzhou. Peng Dehuai, Fang Zhimin, and Su Jingguang, the bandit leaders, personally led the pseudo-37th Army Corps and the 19th and 20th Divisions, taking positions in Bogan and Zuofang, and advancing to Jinxi. On the 12th, they attacked Xuwang via Fengshubu. On the 13th, the southern part of the National Army's 4th Division, Xing Zhennan, advanced diagonally from the border between 　xi and Jinxi, cutting off the bandits' connection with the pseudo-5th Army Corps and blocking their retreat. The National Army, which had retreated 　Xuwang, changed retreat to advance, and attacked the bandits together with Xing's division. From the 13th, the bandits repeatedly charged back and forth near Xuwang, engaging in hand-to-hand combat. The National Army fired their guns and artillery in unison, with bullets raining down. The air force also mobilized, using large bombers loaded with over 120 pounds of bombs, flying over the Jin　area, concentrating fire and bombing the bandits' dense formations. At the same time, a batch of fresh troops was transferred from a certain location and joined the front line, greatly boosting morale. After a fierce battle for a day and night, by noon on the 14th, the National Army had completely annihilated the pseudo-37th Army Corps. The pseudo-19th and 20th Divisions suffered heavy losses and were unable to fight any longer. The remaining bandits retreated in defeat to the southeastern and northeastern borders of Fujian. In total, over 3,000 bandits were killed, over 100 bandits were captured, over 1,000 bandit corpses were left on the battlefield, and over 800 guns and dozens of foreign rifles were seized. The large number of guns captured was the only significant gain since the fifth general offensive. After Jiang received the phone call from Fuzhou, he broadcast a radio message from the headquarters at 8:30 PM on the 14th, reporting on the bloody battles of the 13th and 14th, stating that the 　of Jinxi, the pseudo-37th Army Corps had been completely cut off by our 4th Division, and then fiercely attacked by our various armies near Fengshanbu in Xuwang, killing over 3,000 bandits and seizing over 800 guns. In the future, all officers and soldiers only need to focus on eliminating the pseudo-1st Army Corps to complete the bandit suppression mission, consolidate the national foundation, and comfort the hopes of the Central Government and the people of the whole country. (Evening of November 14th)

The Rise and Fall of the Old and New Factions in Chen Jitang's Army; The Old Faction's Three Armies Seem to Have Lost Power; The New Faction's Divisions Have Increased in Strength 76

Guangzhou Dispatch: Chen Jitang's First Army Group originally had the First, Second, and Third Armies, as well as the Independent First and Second Divisions, and another Guard Brigade. After Li Yangjing, Chief of Staff of the Army Group and Commander of the Third Army, resigned as Chief of Staff, 　a rising military figure, Miao Peinan (formerly under Zhang Fakui), succeeded as Chief of Staff of the First Army Group Headquarters. Chen, with 　Miao's assistance, reorganized military affairs and gradually trained new troops. Those established include the Training Division (师), commanded concurrently by Miao Peinan; the Independent Third Division, commanded by Li Hanhun; and the Independent Fourth Division, commanded by Deng Longguang (Li and Deng were also formerly under Zhang Fakui), forming a new faction system. At the same time, the Independent First Division under Huang Renhuan and the Independent First Division under Zhang Ruigui, directly subordinate to the First Army Group Headquarters, were greatly expanded and reorganized into brigades, with two brigades per division, three regiments per brigade, and one company each directly under the Special Operations, Artillery, Engineering, and Machine Gun units, totaling four regiments and sixteen companies. Each of the above two Independent Divisions expanded to two 　people, exceeding almost half the number of soldiers in the divisions under the Second and Third Armies. 　In addition, the Guard Brigade under Chen Hanguang, directly subordinate to the headquarters, and its affiliated units are equal to the Independent Divisions in strength. Although nominally a brigade, its strength is equal to a division. Therefore, the strength of the troops directly trained and completed by Chen Jitang recently includes four Independent Divisions, one Training Division, and one Guard Brigade, with no fewer than 80,000 soldiers. These newly trained troops are all issued new-style military equipment. As for the old faction's First, Second, and Third Armies, the First Army has been sent far away to southern Jiangxi to engage in bandit suppression, assisting Chen in consolidating the border, already becoming a strong army. The Second and Third Armies are stationed in the Eastern River and along the Jiangxi border. Since Li Yangjing has been recuperating in the provincial capital and has long been away from military affairs, Chen Jitang inspected the Seventh and Eighth Divisions of the Third Army during his recent tour of the Eastern River and then transferred the two divisions to Xunwu area along the Jiangxi border to suppress bandits, placing them under the command of Huang Renhuan, the acting commander of the Second Column. Third Army Commander Li Yangjing's military power has been reduced. Zhang Meixin, commander of the Fourth Division of the Second Army stationed in Xinfeng, was suddenly dismissed from his position recently. Problems have also arisen in the Second Army. Xiang Hanping, commander of the Second Army, seeing such circumstances, has again developed the desire to retire. Although Xiang has not left the province, his intention to resign is firm. Chen Jitang then took back the military power of the Second Army and, 　, assumed the position of commander of the Second Army on the 9th of this month, with Xiang personally handing over the command. After Chen Jitang took over the military power of the Second Army, he ordered Zhang Da, the newly appointed commander of the Fourth Division, to reorganize the troops. The Fifth Division of the Second Army, originally stationed in Huizhou, Heyuan, and Xingning, will be ordered to be transferred to Lianping and Heping, placed under the command of the Second Column, and prepared to go to eastern Jiangxi to suppress bandits. At the same time, the 　Independent Fourth Division under Deng Longguang, stationed in the northern part of the river, was transferred to Huizhou to take over defense. Deng received the order 　business 　returned to the province from Chen on the morning of the 9th to ask for instructions. The troops have also been withdrawn to the province in recent days, taking the Guangzhou-Kowloon train to Huizhou. (November 10th)

Nanhui: Various Public Organizations Oppose the Demarcation of Nanhui-Fengxian Border 79

Various circles in this county oppose the demarcation of the Nanhui-Fengxian border, a long-standing issue that was recently passed by the provincial government meeting. The opposition focuses on a narrow strip of land west of Zhangang Port, east of Qianbu Canal, south of the Huangpu River, and north of Fengxian County, which has been assigned to Fengxian County for administration. The [circles] had previously submitted a request to the Executive Yuan to instruct the provincial government to reconsider. However, it was learned yesterday that the provincial government's appointed commissioner, 　Tang, is scheduled to come to the county on February 15th to oversee the handover procedures. Therefore, various public organizations have once again sent telegrams requesting a postponement of implementation. An emergency meeting on the border issue was convened by the county government. After discussion, it was resolved that although the case had been decided by the provincial government, it should be complied with. However, all public organizations in this county believe that according to the outline of the regulations for the demarcation of Fengxian and Nanhui, based on historical evolution and considering the customs of the people, there are points that should be submitted to the government for　reconsideration. In addition to the fact that various public organizations have directly submitted a request to the Executive Yuan to order the Jiangsu Provincial Government to reconsider, the association should send a letter to the county government to forward it to the provincial government, and the implementation should be temporarily suspended until the Executive Yuan's approval is received.

Nantong: Chenqiao Town Captures Six Bandits in Case 80

Chenqiao was looted by bandits, and the firearms of the stationed security forces were also looted. The county government found out that on the day of the incident, the district chief and security commander Xue Muqing stayed in the city and neglected to provide defense. A deadline of one week was set to solve the case and recover the lost firearms. On the 14th, the district captured six key bandits in the case, including Lu Zhao, Qian Liu, Jin Hai, Na Ni, Lu Sheng, and Miao Wenjun, in Songqiao Township. Two guns were seized, and a security guard named Lü Hongsheng was shot and injured. The bandits were immediately sent to the county government for interrogation that night.

Suzhou: Bizarre Details of Robbery Case in the City 81

After the robbery of three major families in Songxianzhou Lane, Heng Street, the case occurred, the public security bureau sent three suspects to the court, and they have been released on bail. The day before yesterday (14), a patrol officer of the first branch station captured two suspects, Chen A'er and A'wei, and immediately turned them over to the detective team for interrogation. According to the person in charge of the public security bureau, Chen A'er is the main culprit in the case, and all the stolen goods have been transported to Shanghai and hidden in a certain place. A special agent and inspector Huang Zuzeng were dispatched to Shanghai yesterday morning (15) to recover the stolen goods and arrest the fugitives. Public opinion in Suzhou is paying close attention to the case, considering it to be confusing and incomprehensible. Since Tang Kangqi was released on bail, he has left Suzhou.

Wuxi: Barber Kills Student 82

Li Baoyou and his wife, natives of Qingcheng City and Luoshe Town, in the fifteenth district of the county, who were residents of Zhenjiang, opened a barber shop in the town. Baoyou was naturally fierce and often abused the apprentice, Xiao Huazi, (age 20, also from Zhenjiang). The afternoon before yesterday, because he had not washed the rice properly, he beat the back of his head with a club. The apprentice screamed in pain. Neighbors convinced them to stop the fight. The next day, Xiao Huazi could not get out of bed and was very ill. He called a doctor, who said the brain was violently impacted, the blood vessels had burst, and nothing could be done. Not long after, Xiao Huazi died, eyes wide and fists clenched. Residents of the town were outraged and sought to report the matter to the court.

Yangzhou: Elder Brother Injures Younger Brother with Axe for Affair with Sister-in-Law 83

Hu Wu, who pushes a cart for a living, and his wife, who is not content in her chambers, and has long had an affair with his elder brother, Baoyuan. Baoyuan, after having an affair with his sister-in-law, wanted to harm his younger brother. When he and his brother were eating dinner, Baoyuan took his brother unaware and hit his head with a sharp axe, wishing to 　his brother dead. However, as the handle of the axe suddenly broke, he couldn't use his strength, and then he cut his brother's hand. The brother fled. Later, neighbors discovered the wounded man, who was taken to the hospital for treatment. His life is in danger.

Zhenjiang: National Goods Promotion Week Opens 84

Yesterday morning, people from all walks of life in Zhenjiang held the opening ceremony of the National Goods Promotion Week in the auditorium of the county party headquarters. More than 100 representatives from the provincial party headquarters, the provincial government, and various 　groups attended. Chairman Li Qing reported on the necessity of promoting national goods and the significance of holding the promotion week. Three proposals were then passed: (1) Send a letter to the Chamber of Commerce to send all samples of national goods to the Provincial People's Education Hall for permanent display and public viewing. (2) Request the provincial party headquarters and the provincial government to issue separate orders to party members and civil servants under their jurisdiction to 　consume national goods in their entirety. Those who violate this regulation and are reported and found to be true will be severely punished. (3) Notify compatriots across the country to promote national goods in unison. The meeting adjourned at noon.

Hangzhou: Young Man Commits Suicide After Failing to Find Relatives 85

Ji Erchang, a 26-year-old man from Jiangsu, used to work in a newspaper office. Recently, he lost his job and faced financial difficulties. He came to Hangzhou the day before yesterday to visit relatives, but failed to find them. He stayed at the Pinghai Hotel. Because his travel expenses were exhausted, he suffered a severe mental shock. Yesterday (15th) at about 12:00 noon, he went directly to the sixth park by the lake 　and threw himself into West Lake to commit suicide. Patrol officer Bi Yusheng happened to pass by and rescued him ashore. He was barely breathing. He hired a car and sent him to the police station, where Ji gradually regained consciousness.

Huzhou: Police and Bandits Exchange Fire at Wushengmen 86

Dai Shixi, the magistrate of Wuxing County in this city, recently received a letter from the Yu Hang Security Brigade sent by the director of the brigade, Feng Shifan, stating that the bandits were told that the gang leader, Zhou Rongting, and his followers were in Wushengmen Tiger Ridge near Yunchao Mountain in a shack. 　The Magistrate 　reported the crime, and ordered chief of the police station Chen Hongji and Huang Yu ,to bring eight detectives and join with chief police Xu Chengqi and about ten police to the location on the 13th at 4 o'clock. As they entered, a dog suddenly emerged. As the police tried to enter, a dog suddenly emerged barking loudly, and the gang then emerged with guns and began firing upon them, and so the police returned fire. After about an hour, the gang began to retreat, and so the police chased them. Police officer Wang Yuwen was then hit trying to courageously capture a criminal, and was then sent to the city 　　hospital, and at the same time the police attempted to follow them. They did 　capture ten bandits including Zhang Qian, Xue Duolao, Qiu Aying, Qiu Amao, Chen Ajin, Liu Xingyou, Qian Ahai, Dong Zhongxiang, Shen Zhishui, bandit wife Wang Shi, along with a musket, and at 6 pm brought them to the city.
