Shanghai Brewery's Negligence; Part of the Bottle Stopper Factory Burns Down 172

The Shanghai Brewing Company, located at No. 420 Gordon Road, Yichang Road, has been expanding its operations in recent years. Dozens of seven-story cement factory buildings have been added next to the original factory site, and some of the construction has been completed. As such, the factory relocated its bottle stopper manufacturing to the fourth floor of the new building. The procedure for manufacturing bottle stoppers involves first applying heated pitch to a foreign-made utensil, and then applying cork slices to prevent leakage. As such, the workshop contained items such as pitch, cork, and stoves. At 5:00 PM yesterday, after the factory closed, thick smoke suddenly filled the bottle stopper manufacturing room, quickly causing a fire. Furthermore, pitch is an easily combustible substance. Before long, flames burst out from the gaps in the cement walls. Neighbors and guards nearby smelled the pitch and noticed that the cement factory walls had been burned. They rushed to report to the Yichang Road fire department and notified the police. After receiving the news, the fire department rushed to the scene with hose carts to extinguish the fire, but the bottle stopper room had become a fire pit, making it impossible to enter. They then applied water from outside the windows. However, the fire was raging and it was difficult to extinguish at that time. They quickly notified the Central Fire Department and other departments to dispatch vehicles to assist in the firefighting efforts. The fire began to subside at around 6:45 PM and was soon extinguished. However, the interior of the room was reduced to ashes. Fortunately, the walls were made of cement, so other factory buildings were not affected, otherwise the consequences would have been disastrous. The cause of the fire has not yet been determined. However, according to bystanders, it may have been caused by unextinguished ashes. The losses were significant.

Another Fire Reported in Tanzi Bay 173

In recent days, the weather has been dry, and there have been no fewer than six or seven fires in the shacks of the poor in the Zhabei area due to carelessness. Tanzi Bay and Hengfeng Road have been the worst hit, with victims having nowhere to live, resulting in a very tragic situation. Unexpectedly, at 1:15 AM yesterday, another fire broke out in a shack on wasteland to the west of the Tanzi Bay Dayang Bridge. Xu Zaixiang, a Jiangbei native, was engaged in pig farming and built a shack in this area. The night before, after falling asleep, he forgot to turn off the kerosene lamp. While tossing and turning, he knocked the lamp off the table, causing the oil to spill onto the straw, immediately causing a fire that spread quickly. When Xu Zaixiang awoke from his dream, it was already impossible to rescue the situation. He rushed out to call for help, and the neighbors were awakened at the same time, rushing to escape. There was chaos as people shouted and screamed. The police station dispatched from the fourth district, third precinct was informed and immediately dispatched police to the scene to suppress the situation. They also notified the Zhabei fire departments to dispatch vehicles to the scene to extinguish the fire. Fortunately, the rescue was early, and a major disaster was avoided. As a result, more than ten shacks were burned down, and a rental rickshaw company was also affected, suffering significant losses. The fire starter, Xu Zaixiang, was taken to the police station for questioning after the incident and was sent to the General Bureau for investigation yesterday afternoon.

Gambling Den Cracked Down on in Yanhai Road 174

Police officer Wang, of the Second District, First Precinct, along with Qian Jiangyong, were patrolling Yanhai Road at 9:00 AM yesterday when they saw many people entering and exiting No. 27. They realized that it was a lottery operation, collecting gambling money for the morning session. They immediately entered and arrested Wei Jinru (from Danyang), Le Liangchen (from Luan Yang), Lu Yuanliang (from Danyang), Zhou Laosan (from Danyang), Ying Shuguan (from Danyang), and Ying Fushen (from Danyang), a total of six people. Along with them, they seized twelve yuan in gambling money, lottery paper, abacuses, and other items. The police station has requested an investigation. After questioning by Director Shen, the defendants admitted to secretly setting up a gambling operation to lure people into gambling on the lottery to reap huge profits. They were sentenced to be sent to the General Bureau for legal action.

Wuxi Kidnappers Arrested in Shanghai; Renowned Doctor Zhu Yunting Redeemed with Two Thousand Gold Pieces 175

One Kidnapper Arrested After Fleeing with the Ransom

There is a man named Zhu Yunting in Beishikou, Wuxi County, who practices medicine and sells it in his hometown. Many people come to his door seeking treatment, and it is common for nearby villages to invite him. As his income from medical consultations was substantial, his family gradually became wealthy, attracting the attention of bandits who regarded him as a cash cow. They had repeatedly considered kidnapping him but had no opportunity. On September 15th, the bandits sent their accomplices to Zhu's house, pretending to invite him to treat a patient at a certain place, luring Zhu out of his house. After gaining control, they fled. When they arrived at the riverbank near the Qingqi Bridge, a pre-arranged bandit boat was docked. They immediately took Zhu aboard and hid him among the reeds. They then demanded a ransom of 5,000 yuan from his family for his release. After secret negotiations conducted by local officials, the Zhu family safely redeemed Zhu Yunting with 2,000 gold pieces at the Guanyin Temple in Bazibqiao, five miles from the city of Wuxi. After the incident, the Wuxi County Government, after hearing about it, summoned Zhu to the county to inquire about the kidnapping in detail. They also ordered detectives to investigate the bandits' whereabouts within a specified period to eliminate future troubles and ensure the safety of the residents. According to reliable sources, the kidnappers fled to Shanghai after dividing the ransom and mixed into the concession. The county magistrate issued an arrest warrant and sent Wu Zhengrong, the county government police chief, to Shanghai to conduct a strict investigation. On the afternoon prior, he requested the assistance of the Consular Police, and detective Yu Haibo and western detective Black rushed to the Xinlongyuan Tea House at No. 501 Bei Shaanxi Road and arrested Yu Hailin, a native of Wuxi. Yu was taken to the police station for questioning. According to Yu's confession, he admitted that he was involved in the kidnapping and that he received 30 yuan. His other accomplices were hiding at No. 25, Lane 129, Route Pere Robert, in the French Concession. The police rushed to apprehend them, but they found nothing. Yesterday morning, Yu was sent to the First Special District Court, where he was questioned by Judge Wu Ziqi. Police Chief Wu presented an official letter requesting the transfer of custody to Wuxi County Government. When questioned by Wu, Yu did not deny the confession made at the police station. The police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, stated that the police had no objection to the transfer requested by the Wuxi County Government. Judge Wu then approved the transfer of Yu Hailin to Police Chief Wu to be taken back to the Wuxi County Government for trial.

The residence of national medicine doctor Zhu Xiangsheng at No. 17, Lane 27, Yunnan Road caught fire at 3:15 AM yesterday due to carelessness, immediately producing black smoke and flames. Strongman Zha Rui Long's Brothers Withdraw Lawsuit 177

The case of strongman Zha Rui Long being sued by his cousin Zha Rui Lian in the First Special District Court for embezzling inheritance was scheduled for continued hearing yesterday afternoon. Judge Wu Xiangzu opened the fifth criminal court to hear the case. Defendant's lawyer Yuan Yang'an stated first that the defendant had filed a counterclaim against the plaintiff for slander, etc. Judge Wu then transferred the case files from the District Court to the plaintiff's lawyer and asked him to point out the points of embezzlement. After reviewing the case files, the plaintiff's lawyer stated that although there was no evidence of embezzlement by Zha Rui Long in the case files, there was one point: after Zha Rui Long and his sister Xin Yuan reached a settlement, the siblings of the defendant's side had offered 1,000 yuan for marriage expenses, but the money was in the defendant's custody and he refused to hand it over, which was sufficient to prove embezzlement, etc. Subsequently, Judge Wu persuaded both parties to reconcile, stating that since the two parties were brothers, even if there were monetary disputes, they could be discussed and resolved from there, and there was no need to litigate and harm feelings, etc. After considering the matter, the plaintiff agreed to withdraw the lawsuit, and Zha Rui Long also expressed his willingness to withdraw the counterclaim. The court then ruled that the case was not accepted, and the case was concluded.

Physicians Association Requests the Establishment of Autopsy Centers in Nanshi and Zhabei 178

The Shanghai Physicians Association believes that there are no autopsy centers in Nanshi and Zhabei in the Chinese district, and autopsies are often performed on the spot, which not only hinders traffic but also harms public health. Yesterday, they specifically passed a resolution at the autumn general meeting to "request the local authorities to quickly establish autopsy centers in Nanshi and Zhabei to emphasize public safety and public health." The document was submitted to the Municipal Government and the District Court, stating, "Petition for the establishment of autopsy centers in Nanshi and Zhabei, two districts of this city. It is noted that Nanshi and Zhabei are adjacent to the concession, and the International Council has agreed to this. For more than twenty years, local construction and successive clinics have been established, which is a symbol of civilization and progress, and all citizens enjoy the benefits of the community. But if you try to recall, the most important public service, the autopsy center, is still lacking. In the past, it was still possible to excuse it as Zhu Changming of forensic medicine, and there was a lack of specialized talents, and no one dared to move the body lightly, so they had to be examined on the spot. But today, forensic research has its own specialized institutions, and there is no lack of talents. The examination has scientific methods to support it, and there is no need to prohibit the movement of the deceased. Moreover, Shanghai opened up earlier and is the crown of the golden country. In the concession, where bodies are disposed of, there are two autopsy centers, but in the large area of Nanshi and Zhabei, which are surrounded by them and under the sovereignty of our country, there is something lacking. This not only leaves foreigners with reason for scorn, but Shanghai is also affected because there are no autopsy centers. Once a murder occurs, it is bound to cause a sensation, disrupt order, and sometimes expose corpses and flesh, attracting flies and mosquitoes, which hinders hygiene. Even worse, the restriction on moving the body leads to local ruffians, cunning officials, and slippery officials stirring up trouble and extorting money. Innocent people are implicated, and the harm is so great. Our local authorities have also heard about it from time to time. Why has there been no reform to this day? Perhaps this area is impoverished and it is difficult to raise funds, so the discussion has been temporarily postponed. However, the establishment of an autopsy center is related to national image and social order and public health. If this can be delayed, what cannot be delayed? Moreover, how much can it cost to establish one or two autopsy centers? The association has seen this and dares to express its opinion. We request that your government (court) work with the Shanghai District Court (Municipal Government) to quickly plan and select appropriate locations and establish autopsy centers in Nanshi and Zhabei within a specified period to benefit citizens and improve the city's appearance. In addition to the official submission, we respectfully request that you review and implement this for the public good."

Correspondence 190

To the esteemed editor:

Regarding an item in the "Local News" section of yesterday's newspaper, titled "Land Value Tax Assessment Standards, Valuation Review Begins," the final paragraph stated that if landowners had concerns regarding the assessed value, they could, when the tax collection begins next year, go to the land tax collection office in the commercial district, state their reasons, and request corrections. However, this differs from the information released by our bureau. According to Article 6 of the Provisional Regulations for the Collection of Land Value Tax, if a property owner has objections to the announced land value, they must submit a valid reason and apply to the Land Bureau within the prescribed time limit for submission to an arbitrator for arbitration. We hope you will investigate and make the necessary corrections. Respectfully, Shanghai Municipal Land Bureau, Second Division, November 15, 1933.

Ministry of Education Requests Embassies to Collect Film Regulations from Various Countries 193

The Social Education Department of the Ministry of Education, in response to a request from the China Educational Film Association, has sent a letter to embassies stationed abroad, requesting the collection of film censorship regulations from various countries, as well as publications related to film. The original letter stated that the association is an organization dedicated to using film to assist education and promote culture. As China's film industry is developing rapidly, there is an urgent need to compile a film yearbook to understand the past and guide future trends. The yearbook is now being compiled by a committee organized by Chen Lifu, Pan Gongzhan, Wang Pingling, Li Jiaxiang, Li Jingmi, Dai Bi, and Zhang Changren. In addition to detailing the current state of China's film industry, it is planned to include the film regulations of various countries and the organization of film censorship agencies for reference. Therefore, the association is requesting the Ministry's assistance in forwarding a letter to embassies stationed abroad, requesting them to collect the film regulations and related publications from the Ministry of Interior or Education of the countries where they are stationed. The collected publications should be compiled and sent back to China by December of this year to facilitate compilation. We would be grateful. Accordingly, we are writing to request investigation and action and a reply as to the outcome.

New Regulations for Military Training in Nanjing Schools 197

Since taking office, Pan Guqiang, Director of the National Military Education Department of the Training Directorate, has spared no effort in rectifying military training in schools. On the 9th of this month, he summoned more than ten military instructors from Nanjing schools to give instructions, stating that the biggest reason for the failure of military training in schools in the past was that there were too many students and only one instructor per school. Now, in order to remedy this shortcoming, new regulations have been revised. According to the new measures, all instructors in Nanjing schools must jointly take responsibility for military training in all schools, and it is stipulated that these measures will be implemented starting on the 13th. From now on, when military training is conducted in various schools in Nanjing, at least five instructors will be on site to assist.

Dr. Fryer Inspects Jiangsu Provincial College of Education ▲丨 Arrives in Wuxi on the 17th and Stays for Two Days 198

Since the UK agreed to return the Boxer Indemnity funds to China, an organization has been established to promote Sino-British cultural exchange. Recently, the church specially invited Dr. Fryer (female) to come to China to inspect education, hoping to contribute to Sino-British cultural exchange. Dr. Fryer is British and was in charge of important work for the War Zone Relief Committee in France during the European War. From 1919 to 1926, she served as the Honorary Secretary-General of the China Penal Reform Joint Association and is a well-known prison reform expert. From 1926 to 1931, she served as the president of Oxford House. She currently remains an honorary professor at the university. In addition to obtaining a Ph.D. in literature in her early years, she also obtained a Ph.D. in political science from Victoria University. She is also very experienced in educational administration, having worked for the University Economic Committee under the British Treasury Department for many years. In the past few months, Dr. Fryer has inspected education in Beijing and Nanjing and other places in China for many days. The Wuxi Jiangsu Provincial College of Education has long been included in her inspection schedule because the college has achieved remarkable results in running agricultural education and mass education. Moreover, this type of education is a new undertaking in China and should have a significant impact on the women's movement among the people. She will conduct a thorough on-site inspection. It is understood that the doctor is scheduled to visit the college on the 17th of this month and stay at the college for three days to conduct a detailed inspection, paying particular attention to the daily life of the students. She has agreed to give two public lectures. In addition, professors at the college have invited the doctor to attend academic discussions to discuss the actual situation of Chinese education, to conduct collaborative observations, and to be jointly developed by the college. Local News

The Student Unrest at Wuben Girls' School Gradually Subsides ▲ Students Will Respond to Transfer Opinions Today ▲ Director Pan Has Agreed to Allow Two Suspended Students to Return to Class 199

Since the recent student unrest at the Wuben Girls' Middle School in this city, Education Director Pan Gongzhan has been very angry because the students were instigated and willingly exploited. He adopted strict measures, but since Mr. Pan summoned all the staff to a meeting, the faculty and staff have been willing to make adjustments, so the unrest has subsided and can be resolved within days.

▲Situation at the School Yesterday, more than 300 female students, accounting for about three-fifths of the total number, voluntarily went to school. They maintained calm during morning exercises and self-study. Although the Education Bureau sent personnel to monitor the situation, they did not interfere too much. In addition, several female inspectors were on site to prevent any problems. The school was as peaceful as ever yesterday, but students were still not allowed to use the telephones on campus.

▲Withdrawal of Security Team After the unrest at the school the day before, the fifth squadron of the police brigade from the Municipal Public Security Bureau was dispatched to be stationed there. Since the Chief Secretary of the Municipal Government, Yu, accepted the students' request the day before yesterday, the police officers have withdrawn to the Education Bureau. However, as a precaution, more than ten police officers are still stationed at the school gate to protect the school.

▲Mediation by Faculty and Staff The faculty and staff of the school held a meeting with the heads of all levels of the middle school department at 10:00 AM yesterday, gently advising the students and stating the Education Bureau's attitude towards the matter. Although the heads of all levels have accepted the mediation of the faculty and staff, they must still consult the opinions of all the students, so they will respond today.

▲Education Bureau's Attitude Director Pan Gongyan of the Municipal Education Bureau is currently instructing the faculty and staff to persuade the students, hoping that the students will immediately realize their mistakes and not allow the school to be dissolved. Therefore, the Education Bureau did not express anything yesterday, waiting to see how the students will respond today. However, if the students still stubbornly refuse to come to their senses, the Education Bureau will be forced to forcibly remove the students from the school in order to thoroughly rectify the situation.

▲Focus of the Problem The three demands made by the students in this unrest are: (1) Reinstatement of the two suspended students; (2) Removal of Dean of Studies Jiang Wenbao; (3) Restoration of the Student Self-Government Association. Regarding the first item, the Education Bureau has stated that the two students are temporarily suspended and can return to school with a guarantee from their parents if they repent. The third item is not a problem if they can formally organize according to legal procedures and submit a report to the party and government agencies for record. However, the students still insist on the second item, and the Education Bureau absolutely refuses to allow students to interfere in school administration, fearing that it will set a bad precedent. This has become the focus of the problem, and the Education Bureau will have no choice but to take decisive action.

▲Two Students May Return to Class Li Minhua, a temporarily suspended student, was summoned by Director Pan yesterday and went to the Education Bureau accompanied by her parents. Director Pan asked her about her involvement as a representative. According to her, each grade of the student self-government association had two representatives, totaling twenty-four. The first time four representatives requested an interview with Principal Yan, and the second time eight representatives went. She (Li) did not know Dean Jiang, and it was only because the classmates said they did not want him to come that she, as a representative, had to say that. She did not know the reasons. The student's parents were very understanding and, together with Director Pan, enlightened Li, who then realized her mistakes. Director Pan agreed that after the school reopened, her parents could send a letter stating that she had repented, and she could return to school. As for Fang Xiuzhi, another suspended student, because her parents were in Ningbo, her guarantor, Mr. Yan, went to see Director Pan yesterday and stated that it was natural for the student to repent for her mistakes. Fang had always been a good student, and he could guarantee that she would correct any mistakes she had made, now or in the future. Therefore, after the school reopens and Fang submits a letter of repentance, she will also be able to return to school.

Municipal Education Bureau Orders Chinese Girls' Middle School to Close by a Deadline 200

The private Chinese Girls' Junior Middle School applied to the Municipal Education Bureau for approval to establish the school in September of this year. The Education Bureau sent personnel to investigate and found that the principal, department heads, and faculty were not present, and there were no students. Since the school had already enrolled students without permission this semester, there was no need to establish the school. Therefore, the Education Bureau ordered the school to close. Now, the Education Bureau states that the school has not complied with the order to close and is still operating, which is improper. The Education Bureau has ordered the school's board of directors to quickly instruct the school to close down as soon as possible and submit a report for review.

Franco-Chinese University Pharmacy Department Holds Graduation Examination 203

The Pharmacy Department of the Franco-Chinese University on Albert Road in Shanghai was established in 1929 and is the only pharmacy university in China. Its first class of students could have graduated in the summer of this year. However, the school emphasizes rigorous training for its students. In addition to the entrance examination each year, fourth-year students must also pass four graduation examinations. Yesterday (the 14th) was the fourth graduation examination. In advance, local health agencies were invited to send personnel to supervise the examination to show caution. Apart from the Health Bureau, which was unable to send personnel, over ten people attended, including Dr. Barry Smith, representative of the French Consulate, Dr. Zhu Xiangying, representative of the Chinese Medical Association, and Dr. Libaud, Director of the Health Department of the French Municipal Council. They were seated together with the professors of the school. In addition to answering the questions of the professors, the examinees were asked to answer questions raised by the proctors on the spot. The students were able to answer fluently, and the proctors, such as M. Le Plomb, Dr. Libaud, expressed great satisfaction. The results of this examination have been announced. The graduates are Wang Dian ____, Ye ____ Qiu, Dai Kai, Wu Yuwan, Zhang Rui, He ____ San, Hua Lanchou, Chen Houbei, and Hou ____ ____, a total of nine people. The school has decided to send the first five to the University of Lyon in France to continue their studies for further education.

Children's Intellectual Development Society Raises Funds to Establish Free Night School for Commoners 204

The Shanghai Commoners' Children's Intellectual Development Society has made great efforts to promote commoners' education over the years. However, it feels that the shortage of funds prevents it from developing and popularizing education. The society, in view of the large number of commoners who have dropped out of school, has decided to establish a free night school for commoners to provide more opportunities for further education for those who have dropped out of school and to allow unemployed young people in the vocational world to receive remedial education. Previously, a grand carnival was held to raise funds, and all the proceeds were used for the free night school for commoners. The date has been set for the 15th of this month and will be held at the Kade Grand Theater in Xinzha. It is said that the performance program on that day includes dramas, harmonica, singing, dancing, and comedies by the Chunhua Drama Society. It is expected that there will be a grand occasion at that time.

Hao Gengsheng's Talk in Jinan 208

(Jinan Correspondence) Hao Chengsheng, Professor of Physical Education at National Shandong University in Qingdao, was recently hired by the Ministry of Education as a Physical Education Supervisor. He arrived in Jinan yesterday from Qingdao and will take a train to Beijing at 9:00 AM today (the 14th) to take office. The reporter met Mr. Hao on the train as he was leaving Jinan and inquired about everything. Mr. Hao said that since the National Games, the people of the country have generally understood the importance of physical education, so the Ministry of Education hired him as a supervisor and he is going to take office. As for how to promote physical education in the future, there are no specific methods yet, and he will discuss it with various physical education experts. The position of physical education professor at Shandong University that he held has been taken over by Mr. Song Fu, and someone is also responsible for the Qingdao Stadium, and so on.

Friendly Football Match: Youyou Defeats Western Captives 209

▲Result: 4 to 3

The Youyou Football Team played a friendly match against the Western Captives Team yesterday at the Zhonghua Baseball Field, with two to three thousand spectators. The two teams had similar skills and the situation was even. In the first half, each team scored two goals, and there was no clear winner. In the end, Youyou won 4 to 3.

▲Each Scored One Goal. The Western Captives kicked off and attacked first, repeatedly penetrating Youyou's territory. Youyou defended strictly, making it difficult for the opponent to get close. After a long stalemate, Zhu mistakenly kicked the ball into the center of the goal within the defense line, giving Defei an easy goal to open the scoring, with Youyou unfortunately conceding the first goal. The whole army was inspired and strived for progress. Sun Xishun rode forward, and Zhong Yongsen raided the camp alone, resulting in a 1-1 tie. Shen Bai sent troops to the border, and Zhong Yongsen revisited the old place. Western Captives' goalkeeper Bochi received and then lost the ball. Zhong lightly tapped it, taking the lead with a score of 2-1. The Western Captives launched a fierce counterattack. Wokele coordinated in the middle, and Gengensheng pounced like a hungry tiger. Qi Yongchun handled the situation improperly, allowing Huo Gengensheng to push his stomach in, resulting in a 2-2 draw.

▲Youyou Wins. After resting and re-engaging, eight minutes later, Sun received assistance from Chen Jiaqiu and Li Shuoyou and shot at an angle, and the enemy's goal was lost again. Youyou once again took the lead, but just as they gained in the mulberry field, they lost in the elm field. The Western Captives' forwards advanced step by step, besieging Youyou. After a long struggle between the two sides, Gengensheng secretly crossed the Chencang pass, shot but missed, and met it with his head, finally knocking open the goal, making it a 2-2 draw. Youyou was eager to win and continued to work hard, invading the enemy's camp. Zhong Yongsen took advantage of the opponent's goalkeeper dribbling the ball and unexpectedly kicked it into the net, making it 4-2, giving Youyou the victory. After that, the two armies fought fiercely, and Youyou stepped up their defense to maintain the situation.

Special Announcement

A General Overview of Modern Chinese Educational Thought (II) 214

Lecture by Shu Xin cased, Notes by Sun Yucai

▲The Scope of the Modern Era and the Greatness of the Modern Era

The history of education is as long as that of humanity itself. Therefore, all human history contains the history of educational thought. The "modern era" I am referring to starts from the first year of the Tongzhi reign in the Qing Dynasty to the present. Why do I define it in this way? Because since the establishment of the Tongwen Guan in Beijing that year, the educational system that had evolved over thousands of years in Chinese history gradually began to be replaced by the Western educational system, and the traditional ideas associated with it were gradually destroyed without any remainder. If we compare the educational phenomena of the sixty years after the establishment of the Tongwen Guan with those of the sixty years before its establishment, we will find that they are not only completely different in form but also completely different in content. Moreover, because of all the major problems that have occurred in the world in the past seventy years, such as the Industrial Revolution, that is, the emergence of mechanical industry, since this mechanical monster was produced, handicraftsmen have naturally been eliminated. According to a survey by proponents of technological politics in the United States, a machine with 14,000 horsepower can equal the power of 90,000 people. In 1833, a bricklayer could only produce 450 bricks per day, whereas now, he can produce 400,000 bricks per day. Another example is a cigarette-making machine, which can produce 2,500 cigarettes per minute, and a light bulb-making machine, which can produce 150,000 light bulbs per day. What do these facts illustrate? They show that with a 30,000 horsepower machine and one worker to manage it, 89,999 people will lose their jobs. With a brick-making machine and one worker to manage it, 8,887 people will lose their jobs. The same is true for the light bulb industry and the cigarette industry. The power of machinery is so great that productivity has been greatly increased. However, consumption is still so limited. As a result, international capitalist imperialists, due to overproduction in their own countries, have been competing to colonize overseas markets. China, with its vast territory and large population, is a place where everyone wants to trade. As a result, since then, China has opened its borders, and its economic system has been reformed. According to relevant statistics, the trade deficit was 80 million yuan the year before last, and it increased to 100 million yuan last year. This means that the silver and money of our country are flowing out in large quantities. How can the people's property and the rural economy not be bankrupted? Due to the occurrence of the Industrial Revolution craze, the social situation in China has gradually affected the villages from the cities. Bankruptcies and unemployment have increased by the thousands, leading to the situation we have today. Naturally, at the same time, this has also affected the changing layers of educational thought.

▲The Purpose of Studying Modern Educational Thought

The new education in China over the past seventy years can truly be said to have been groping in the dark. Although it has cost a lot of manpower and money to earnestly seek a way out, it has still not found a smooth and broad road. The confusion in the intellectual community has only become more serious since the introduction of Western learning. According to statistics from the Ministry of Education the year before last, there are a total of 8.8 million elementary school students in China. If they study for six years, wouldn't there be at least one million graduates each year? What do these one million elementary school graduates do? They simply put on long gowns and look for consumer jobs that don't require manual labor. Children in the countryside are now rarely willing to farm, carry burdens, or cook. There are more than 400,000 middle school students. If they study for six years, there are about 60,000 graduates each year. What do these 60,000 middle school graduates do? Naturally, they follow the example of elementary school graduates, but with an added layer. As for college students, it goes without saying that they are even more like young masters and bureaucrats. This year, there are more than 1,000 college graduates in Shanghai. As far as I know, less than 20% or 30% have found jobs. As a result, everyone has no way out and no solution. However, people have to eat. As Mencius said, "Food and sex are human nature." The current situation is that many people in the intellectual community have nothing to eat, so naturally there will be trouble. No wonder the whole society is filled with extreme squeezing and extreme panic. Squeezing and pushing, you squeeze me, and I squeeze you, and it never seems to get on the right track. To save China, the most important thing now is to stabilize the social order and solve the people's livelihood problems. Now that we understand the situation in society and the education world, I will now talk about the purpose of studying modern educational thought. Educational thought contains extremely complex issues. It is very difficult to understand them all. Even if we understand them clearly, we know that education is not an independent social activity. Everything is subject to the limitations of other social activities. Even if there is a perfect plan, it cannot be realized by education itself. Therefore, the purpose of our study of educational thought is:

(1) To use the concept of historical evolution to prove that all kinds of educational thought are the best solutions to cope with the environment and solve problems at the time. They are not universal truths that everyone can create, and they do not necessarily have to be copied from foreign countries. (2) To use objective facts to prove that educational thought is produced by educational practice. The actual situation in society is the source of thought. In studying the history of thought, we must not abandon the facts and engage in empty talk. (3) To seek out the causes and consequences of modern Chinese educational thought from historical evidence to provide some materials for creating new education suitable for China. (4) To seek evidence from history to prove that education is not an independent social activity and is often subject to other phenomena, so that educators will strive to transform society in addition to education.

(Thought) Now that we have gained a general understanding of "educational thought" and the "scope and purpose of the modern era," let us now turn to the history of thought itself.

Spring and Autumn

A Kind of Funeral Worth Introducing 215

— Yan Qiao

I once saw a funeral procession in Jinan, with a band of stilt performers in the middle of the procession. When they reached a lively intersection, everything stopped to watch the stilt performance. I almost thought it was a competition. In Suzhou, I often heard people who loved to watch the excitement boasting about when a certain family would have a "grand send-off of the coffin." I never understood what the meaning of this kind of funeral was or what it had to do with the deceased.

Even the management of the funeral, the ancestral tablet consecration ceremony, the opening of the mourning hall, the public memorial service, and the extravagance of the selection of the date, friends and relatives are also "going through the motions." Confucius said, "Eating beside a mourning house, one does not get full." I regret that he was not born today, otherwise he would surely be able to feel "both drunk and full" every time. This kind of funeral is common among the middle class, as if not doing so would mean not following the rites and wearing mourning properly.

Now there is a funeral that is very different. Instead of going to the countryside to build a grave and dig a pit, the deceased is buried in Anle Garden [the Christian cemetery in Suzhou]. At 2:00 PM the day before, there is a family memorial service, and at the same time, local people hold a memorial meeting in their home. Even the obituary is very unique, divided into three categories: eulogies from friends and relatives, elegies, and mourning announcements, encompassing classical Chinese, vernacular Chinese, rhymed prose, and new poems.

The mourning announcement mentions the deceased's virtues, and two things are worth introducing: one is the opening of the family library, and the other is the establishment of an ancestral memorial hall. On the anniversary of the ancestors' death, the practice of monks and Taoists performing repentance ceremonies and chanting scriptures is abolished, and paper ingots and funerary objects are not used. Only a bunch of fresh flowers and a stick of incense are placed in front of the ancestors' portraits and relics. After the children bow in respect, the head of the family explains in detail the ancestors' entrepreneurial endeavors and daily deeds. Everyone silently commemorates them. The traditional etiquette of "worshiping gods as if gods were present" is abolished. This kind of reform, which considers both Chinese and foreign practices and integrates ancient and modern customs, is something we have all thought of, but we have never had the courage to implement.

Finally, I want to explain who is in charge of this funeral. Speaking of it, many people may know, it is Mr. Xu Chuanming, who served as the president of the Southeast Industrial Bank and was elected as a member of the National Assembly. His mother, who observed chastity and raised her children alone, passed away. The Xu family in Suzhou is considered wealthy. If they had "failed to avoid vulgarity," they would have at least made a big fuss for several days. Who would have known that it would be so simple? Isn't it worth introducing to today's society, which is full of vanity? I also hope that "a part of the industry will be used for a rural cooperative venture" (see Hu Bolun's Eulogy). That this statement can be realized in the shortest possible time, then his filial piety will be even greater.

A Record of a Candidate's Self-Description 216

— Qing Qu

Two days ago, I happened to meet a gentleman at a banquet who had returned from the recent college entrance examination in the capital. He seemed like one of those newly rich gentlemen. I asked another friend for his name and surname, and I understood it very clearly. However, I cannot write it out, lest I hurt the loyal and honest. This must be declared first. On the surface, this gentleman is indeed extraordinary, exceptionally handsome, and indeed a fashionable figure. Therefore, his conversation is also witty and humorous, often making people laugh. However, he inevitably has the disappointed attitude of Liu Kui, who failed the examination and earned the sadness of a hero. At that time, there were no less than thirty or forty people gathered together and drinking heavily. His every word and sentence made people listen attentively and become silent. It can also be seen that although this examination is not like the former provincial or metropolitan examinations, the general public's desire for vanity has not changed!

He said: "I made quite a fool of myself in this examination. When I was studying at a certain middle school, no matter how eloquently the teacher lectured in the classroom, I would still leisurely read a novel once or twice. Sometimes I would twist peanuts in one hand and peel Liangxiang chestnuts in the other, munching them. Sometimes I would simply rest my head on my arms and sleep. When the bell rang and woke me from my afternoon dream, drool would be streaming down the desk. I would hastily flip through a few books as a show, and then go to another class. Later, I actually got into college, but my laziness in studying and my fear of using my mind became even more serious. Whenever there was opposition to exams, I would always be the first to propose it and organize a strike alliance with the school authorities, fighting until one of us won. This was less than ten years ago. Unexpectedly, now, not only do I not oppose it, but I am willing to go to the examination hall to suffer. Thinking about it, I don't even know why!"

"Alas! At first, I thought this kind of examination would be very convenient. How could I know that the examination officials would ask such difficult questions? Just take the Chinese language question, 'If there are no legalist advisers when entering the country, and no foreign enemies when leaving the country, the country will surely perish.' When I received it, I really couldn't remember. Righteous men, brave men, warriors, strong men, Avalokiteśvara, my father is a gentleman in our hometown, and I have never seen a 'legalist adviser.' How do you expect me to explain the word 'adviser'? Moreover, now that there are 'foreign enemies,' our country is probably going to perish, but it says, 'If there are no foreign enemies, the country will surely perish.' Perhaps 'surely' can be interpreted as 'not,' but if not, how do you expect me to write? And what about 'Yellow Turbans' and 'taking officials as teachers,' these history questions are things I have never stored in my mind. Therefore, although I entered the examination hall this time, I can be considered to have let out a fart in the examination hall, which can be considered as having won a breath for my ancestors." As he spoke, he had a completely arrogant,眉飛色舞 posture, and the listeners were all giggling and laughing.

Women and Wine 217

— Bing Ding

Wine is life's "comfort" and "stimulant." Therefore, poets, artists, novelists, heroes, beauties... almost all like wine. Women are also life's "comfort" and "stimulant," and have the same effect as wine.

Wine has different flavors, and so do women. The natural charm and gentle elegance of a village girl is like the local Shaoxing Huadiao wine. It is not that there are no beautiful and quiet women in the city, but they are somewhat like the Shaoxing wine sold in liquor stores, with some "water" mixed in. Modern women are like champagne. When the cork is first opened, bubbles burst out, which is very beautiful and trendy, but when you taste it, it is bitter after all. How can it intoxicate people? Village women, spending a lot of money on makeup and imitating others, are like white liquor water. Although some friends from Jiangbei get drunk after drinking it, it cannot be compared with Huadiao and Jingzhuang. As for foreign wines such as brandy and whiskey, we are not used to drinking them. Perhaps they have a different flavor, for overseas students who are reading and courting foreign wives to savor the exotic taste.

From foreign wine costing dozens of yuan a bottle, Jingzhuang, Taidiao, Huadiao, mung bean shochu, almond shochu, Jianquan wine... to white liquor water costing fourteen cents a jin, there are countless kinds of wine. Women are the same. "Smelly shrimp matches smelly vinegar." "Beauty is in the eye of the beholder." Wine can intoxicate people, and women can also intoxicate people. Their nature and function are generally the same.

When women drink wine, their almond cheeks blush, and their starry eyes shimmer, naturally making them even more beautiful. Wine can intoxicate people, and women can also intoxicate people. Women plus wine, of course, can intoxicate people even more. In his later years, Lord Xinling used "rich wine" and "women" to end his political life. When heroes grow old, they are so bored, and heartbroken people have unspeakable secrets!

Sunrise on the Bund 218

— Chen Liang

Early morning, the streetlights still emitted a dim glow in the haze, some dust particles rolled along the military trajectory, a layer of white frost covered the patrolmen shrinking in the corners, yawning, they glared and saw one, following behind that fresh fish monger’s pole, reaching out to steal, a pretty big one... he deliberately closed his eyes.

On the steps in front of the Swire Company, several vagrants slept wrapped in advertising paper, with a box of cigarettes and a box of matches as usual beside their heads, smoke from the big steamship drifted out of the iron chimney, drifting to the other side of the Pudong sky, and then faded. The sky on that side must be showing different colors, deep blue, grayish-white, tender yellow, tiger yellow, light red... gradually, gradually, clusters of crimson morning clouds stretched out their arms.

Standing on the floating dock, taking a look at the turbid river, the eyes blurred.

The outlines of the buildings on the opposite bank slowly emerged from the smoke, behind that row of billboards were the high and low jetties, and the morning clouds rose into the sky from behind those jetties, half the sky was dyed red by it, the river water was also dyed red by it, rushing like blood.

The ferrymen were probably still in their dreams.

Perhaps, the eastern sky was about to explode, looking at the serious form, the rapid change. The lights along the Bund were all drooping their eyes, not daring to look at the commotion when night and day exchanged. But, the sun finally came out covered in blood, overlooking the earth, laughing proudly, suddenly shaking, and then falling into the river, falling into pieces, pieces following the turbid river.

At this time, there was a white sun in the sky, the lights were useless.

Crowds began another day of survival and labor.

Short News: Zhang Jun's reputation for "Pillow Green Grass Hall" is passed down through the world. It almost overshadows his reputation as a novelist. This cool autumn, he is eager to express his great spirit with ink. From today onwards, Chen Yan will be at Liangchen Friends Society at the intersection of Beijing Road and Zhejiang Road. From 3:00 to 6:00 pm every day, he will wave his pen for guests, reducing the fee by half, and donating rice paper, exempting ink fees, in order to make a connection with calligraphy and painting.

The Northeast Fourth Company Commander 219

— Zhang Henshui

Episode 18: Gaze Tenderly, Offer Tea, Console Husband in Sorrowful Wedding; Hastily Leave the Border, Forcibly Smile and Bid Farewell to Family

Walking halfway, Yin Deren quietly held Zhao Zizhang's hand and said: "Do you have any feelings?" Zhao Zizhang said: "What feelings do I have? Everyone is the same!" Yin Deren shook his head and smiled: "I am not the same, you can't say that in general. At this time, you realize that it's better to be single." Tian Qing said: "I'm also single, why am I not as happy as you?" Yin Deren smiled: "Are you pretending? Is your being single really clean? Isn't that Ms. Huang a flower that grows on a bare branch? It doesn't matter if the flower that has bloomed is thrown away. This flower hasn’t even been seen what color it is, and it's discarded, which makes people reluctant to part!" Saying that, he patted Zhao Zizhang's shoulder again. What could he say, he could only smile at them. Guan Yaowu was behind the three of them, not saying a word, but sighing heavily. Yin Deren said: "Old Guan, why are you sighing?" Guan Yaowu said: "You are talking about flowers, I don't care, I just can't bear to leave my nest of children." Yin Deren said: "That's still the same, it's better to be single. If you were single from the beginning, how could you have this nest of children?" The four of them were talking, and they had already returned to their respective company headquarters. Zhao Zizhang saw that the lights were all on, so he didn't dare to delay, he first ran to the big kitchen to ask the cooks to make pancakes, the food for more than a hundred people a day was naturally enough to make. After watching for a while, he returned to the company headquarters to supervise the soldiers to pack their small luggage (note: medicine and bullets). In between, he went to the battalion headquarters twice to report to the battalion commander. It can be said that he did not sleep that night. According to the order, they were to gather at the parade ground at seven o'clock to depart. Zhao Zizhang got up at five o'clock. After hurriedly eating breakfast, it was not yet six o'clock. Naturally, the soldiers got up earlier than him. At this time, although the days were long and the nights were short, the sky was still only grayish-white at a little after five o'clock. (241)

Wandering in the Arts

Research on the Soul of Peking Opera 220

— Hu Tiwei

Peking Opera today is declining and falling, on the verge of bankruptcy, which is an undeniable fact, so some people have risen to study the reasons for this decline and the ways to revive it.

Some blame the popularity of mythical and lotus platform plays, but can the theater continue to schedule them if the audience doesn't attend? Some say it is the result of the intrusion of movies in recent years. This seems to say that it's not my fault, it's just that other people are better than me. Does that make sense? So none of these are accurate diagnoses.

In my humble opinion, the biggest fatal wound in the current decline of Peking Opera is the lack of a "soul". Compared to that time, it's like what Yuan Zicai said, "true nature." For example, the leading actors in the current Peking Opera world are undoubtedly Yu Shuyan and Mei Lanfang. If these two famous actors co-star in a "South Heaven Gate", it is sure to cause a sensation and fill the theater. Everyone has to admit that this play is a perfect match. It can be said that the appearance is beautiful, the singing is excellent. But I want to ask a question: For those who have seen their "South Heaven Gate", has your soul ever felt the suffering of the master and servant on stage? Have you ever shed a tear of sympathy for Miss Cao, who is as hurried as a homeless dog and as busy as a fish that escaped the net? If you say you haven't, then this play is equivalent to not being performed, and the audience is equivalent to wasting time, getting nothing at all.

That is to say, the theater a hundred years ago, although it was a crude stage show with chaotic jumps and shouts, each play had a meaning of loyalty, filial piety, and integrity, which could implicitly hold the supreme authority, and was widely imprinted on the minds of the people. This point is what I call the soul of the theater. Now Peking Opera has slowly degenerated and become a pastime for a few idle classes. No matter if they are amateur performers or professionals, as soon as they open their mouths, they either say that this word has a Hubei accent, or that this tune is in the Tan style or the Yu school, as if the essence of the play is only in the singing, and everything else is trivial. We must understand that the most important skill for an actor is to first grab the audience's emotions as soon as they appear on stage, and then try to express the theme of the play as much as possible, so that the audience can get a correct impression. If the actor can't grab the audience's emotions, no matter how correct the pronunciation or how perfect the tune, it's just a musical film in a movie. If the script has no theme, it is empty and decayed, and it will inevitably fail. We must also understand that what is needed today is definitely not just theater that is pleasant to the ear for the idle class, but theater that can help social education and guide the people. Therefore, in addition to the professionals in the Peking Opera world who study theater for the sake of livelihood, all amateur performers, professionals, and even the people who have had a slight interest in theater should stand up to support and promote theater with a soul.

In short, each play itself must first have a sound theme, and each actor must first be skilled in and rich in stimulating and sincere inner performance. Combining these two beauties can live up to the mission of assisting social education. The single-act plays that are popular now are fragmented and broken, and are really unacceptable. On the one hand, we should promote the original good complete plays, and on the other hand, we should compile new plays that are needed today (such as "Lasting Regret of the Late Ming Dynasty" and "Soul Wrongfully Accused," which are plays with a soul). We should use the rich emotions that Peking Opera uniquely possesses to assist social education. Then, I believe that Peking Opera can survive forever, and will not be eliminated by movies, dramas, slapstick, and other kinds of entertainment. The phonetics of every word and sentence, the small body movements of a fleeting glance or a flick of the beard, and even the study of a pair of boots or a blue and white robe, I think are local and trivial issues, we might as well open up a bit more and discuss them later.

Initial Decline Followed by Increase in Food and Flour 236

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, the market for each month showed an initial decline followed by stabilization. With wheat quotations, Chicago did not fluctuate much, and Canada was better by two or three cents. Because of the residual effect of the continuous transactions of wheat the day before, the market atmosphere was particularly unstable. Opening prices were about two cents lower compared to the previous day. However, because the actual factories did not increase prices, the market gradually stabilized after the second round of trading. The speculative groups in the market took advantage of the small purchases, and the customer groups also slightly absorbed, resulting in a positive outlook in the short term. When the market opened in the afternoon, the quotation of Tianjin's current flour was better by one cent, totaling 2.233 yuan. The Shanxi and Yingkou groups also had December transactions. Therefore, the opening prices of each month still rose. According to the current situation, in the short term, the withdrawal of current flour will not be too small. In the long term, due to the easing of the U.S. exchange rate, it is conducive to the ordering of wheat, and there may be many changes in the future. National Goods Weekly of Shen Bao

A Word of Contribution

Three Treasures of National Goods 245

— Yang Mang

Good Quality | Low Price | Comprehensive Service

Mencius said: "The treasures of the princes are three: land, people, and governance." One day, a reporter happened to pass by a company on Nanjing Road and suddenly saw six large characters displayed prominently. Therefore, imitating Mencius's words, he got a sentence: "The reporter said, the treasures of national goods are three: quality, price, and service." Mencius's words have Zhu Xi to annotate them. The reporter's words can only be explained by himself with a thick face.

(1) Quality In the past, there was a saying, "Even if it's broken, it's always Hangzhou goods." Because the people of Hangzhou manufacture goods with the true color of "Hangzhou iron head," which is very reliable. Selecting authentic materials and using real craftsmanship to pursue exquisite products is worthy of admiration. Therefore, for national goods factories to develop their business and for their products to become popular, the first thing is to pursue exquisite materials. Crude and shoddy products are not good business. Changed products are not heroes. Only pursuing the quantity of products and not the quality is not the policy that manufacturers should take.

(2) Price When the quality is good, the price must be appropriate. National goods having excellent quality is the duty of national goods factories. Never raise prices arbitrarily because of the good quality, or take advantage of the year of national goods promotion to profit from it and raise prices very high, causing those who love to use national goods to hesitate or buy with disappointment. I often say: Of course, doing business is about making money and getting rich, but making money and getting rich should not be measured on customers. It is still necessary to focus on the manufacturing side. How can raw materials be cheaper, how can labor be saved, how can consumption be reduced, and how can the output be increased? If you can put effort into this, the price will naturally be low, customers will naturally gather, and sales will naturally expand.

(3) Service I ran to a company sincerely wanting to pick a few kinds of national goods, but the clerks were lazy, rigid, and harsh. They answered one sentence for every two sentences asked, and half a sentence for every sentence asked. They seemed lifeless and impatient to deal with me, exchanging my enthusiasm for their coldness. Then, even if I had twelve points of enthusiasm for using national goods, I could only thank them for their kindness and go elsewhere. Alas! Are these clerks having any grudges against national goods? Can you bear to do this? I ask you, what are you eating? You are the customers of your food and clothing parents. Can you bear to neglect them like this? Then, you should go home, accompany your wife, and hold your son. You don't need to stay in the national goods company to be a molecule who hates national goods. One day, Feng Zhongqing told me: His wife initially did not want to buy anything at a company, but a clerk took out one thing and another, speaking vividly and with great relish. Mrs. Feng was very satisfied and bought dozens of yuan of goods. In fact, the budget was at most two or three yuan. With this clerk who provided comprehensive service, she bought twenty times more goods. Clerks should be like this to be qualified. But the thing to say back is, the current level of living is getting higher and higher, and general clerks feel that they are struggling to support their families and feel that the treatment is meager. Therefore, they are not happy to do things. In fact, managers have eyes. If you work hard, you will definitely not suffer in the future. Moreover, after the business develops, the company makes money, and the bonus for clerks will definitely be a lot. It is up to the clerks themselves to do it. Complaining about others and neglecting customers is deceiving others and taking the blame.

National Goods, Talk

Women and National Goods 246

— Ci Yun

This year is the National Goods Year, the National Goods Year in the midst of national crisis.

In the minds of the general bourgeois ladies, there are no national goods at all. Everything they use must be authentic foreign goods, because they think that foreign goods must be good and fashionable. This is really a psychology of national subjugation.

National goods companies have posted huge advertisements, and the gentlemen who promote national goods are enthusiastically shouting, "Chinese people use Chinese goods!" But they don't pay any attention and are only looking for what foreign goods have arrived in Shanghai.

Poor people certainly don't have the money to buy foreign goods. Even cheap and high-quality domestic goods, they don't have the money to buy. They sell their labor for a living and struggle all day long. It is already very difficult not to be hungry. The things they use are old and broken, so they have to use them for a while.

Ladies! For the sake of the country and the national crisis, you should break this vain psychology, embrace the principle of using only national goods, realize yourself, and persuade your friends to use national goods as well. Then, at least give foreign goods a huge blow and give national goods a powerful help.

Where Does the Failure of National Goods Lie? 247

— Meng Zhao

Speaking of the National Goods Year and comparing it to reality, no one denies that it is extremely painful. The National Goods Year... is just a good-sounding term?

However, why have national goods failed to this point? Silk factories are closed, foreign rice is prevalent, silk sales are sluggish. For everything, we only see foreign goods raising their heads. What about national goods? It is like an abandoned woman wandering on the wrong path. I would like to ask: If this continues, will this abandoned woman still live?

To explore the root cause, we should know where its root is. If we understand the root cause, then we can prescribe the right medicine. As far as I know, there are several points:

(1) It is Speculative Remember the European War era, silk, yarn, and factories sprang up like mushrooms. Regardless of the quality of the products, they accelerated production to make money. They did not care about the strength of their capital. Before long, the war clouds dissipated, and silk, yarn, and factories were completely defeated, resulting in today's miserable modern era. Other manufacturing industries also have a speculative mentality. If you want a business to not fail, how can you get it?

(2) It is Lack of Perseverance Creating national goods, one failure, and you are discouraged and sigh. You have no perseverance to struggle. Or a national goods business fails, and you go to change to another kind of national goods. You don't want to already failed businesses to seek their final victory.

(3) It is Trapped in Finance Bank bosses choose to lend to so-called good brands that do not worry about economic turnover, and accommodate their customers. If they encounter a talent who invents national goods and wants to borrow money to create, they don't even talk about wanting money. Even if it is a factory that has become a great business, they can discuss how much money to use if the market is good. If they encounter a slump, they reject people thousands of miles away and are unwilling to help people in times of crisis, and expect them to revive and get a prosperous business. Those gentlemen have short-sightedness and do not think that they themselves also have the responsibility to promote national goods. This is why national goods have hope, but fail because the financial resources are not provided...

(4) It is Accommodation National goods are not good and should be improved. Manufacturers must not disregard the quality of the goods and blindly accommodate customers, causing them to be despised. Even good national goods will be affected in the same way, eventually leading to failure!

National Goods Marriage 248

— Tian Ran

Recently, people in Shanghai have implemented Mussolini's doctrine, and marriage is very popular. At the end of last month, it was said that there were about three thousand marriages in one day. Blind fortune tellers chose this auspicious day, and three couples became certified in one day. They also had to invite a witness. But I was also very busy. Counting on my fingers, I witnessed five marriages in one month. People said, what is the point of being a witness? I said there is nothing else. I did a great job when I witnessed the marriage, and it was also a promotion of national goods. You think that people come to weddings to eat happy wine and catch up with the excitement. There are old ladies, young ladies, young misses, country girls, and modern women. Eating happy wine is secondary. The first thing is to watch the wedding, look at the bride and groom, and also look at the witness and listen to the witness's words. At that time, I said a word, and they heard a word in their ears. It was really a good opportunity to instill ideas. I said:

The bride and groom wore national goods clothes to get married. This kind of national goods marriage is the most valuable. (Applause) In the future, in the new room and in the new family, everyone should check whether there are any foreign goods or enemy goods? (Applause) The bride must remember! In the future, the most beautiful clothes are national goods clothes. (Applause)

In the future, if the groom buys foreign goods or enemy goods, the bride can go on strike in the new room. (Applause)

In the future, if the bride buys foreign goods or enemy goods, the groom can cut off the economic supply. (Applause)

Little sisters and little brothers, listen! In the future, the first condition for engagement is whether you can implement the use of national goods? (Applause)

National Goods Discussion

How to Increase the Efficiency of Promoting National Goods? 249

— Ba Ling

"Promote national goods," "Promote national goods." This movement has been carried out vigorously several times, but what is its effect? Where is the achievement it has shown? This is a question that deserves our doubt.

"Promote national goods," why can't it achieve great results? There are many reasons for this, but the fact that those at the top cannot lead by example, and that the people of the country despise government orders and do not implement them, are the main reasons. There is no doubt about this!

Now, the author humbly offers a few suggestions below. If they can be implemented effectively, the national goods movement will surely have a huge effect. And these articles and several meetings will have greater results.

(1) Government authorities and public officials of various agencies must use national goods. Those who violate this will be dismissed. (Except for those who have no national goods to use.)

(2) Agencies and organizations must purchase national goods. Those who violate this must be ordered to compensate the purchaser, and those who violate this more than twice will be dismissed. (This method is practiced in Japan and has achieved great results.)

(3) School teachers and staff must purchase national goods for their supplies. Those who violate this will be dismissed if 100% of the materials used are not Chinese materials.

(4) Party staff must use national goods for their supplies. Those who violate this will be expelled from the party.

The above four points seem too strict on the surface, but if they can be earnestly implemented, the national goods movement will have a satisfactory result. However, the most important point is that government authorities, public officials, party staff, and school teachers and staff can lead by example. Then, there may be great effects to be received. Confucius said: "When those above have a good preference, those below will surely have a greater preference." This is a very good motto.

National Goods Introduction

Shortcomings and Improvements of National Goods Rice Hulling Machines 250

— Zhu Zhenmu

In the previous issue of this journal, there was an article about the introduction of rice hulling machines. Now, the reporter has more opinions on the shortcomings and improvements of the machine, and is willing to publish them in this journal. I hope that the manufacturing companies will study and improve it, which is also a way to promote national goods. Let's list the shortcomings and improvement methods below:

▲ Current Shortcomings of the Machine

Although the movement and connection of the machine are good, there are still many shortcomings. Now, the reporter will add a judgment as far as he can reach: (1) There is no shield in front of the machine, so the grains under the track are scattered all over the field, and it takes effort to collect them again. (2) Because of the huge piercing force of the nails, short and thin rice straw is often mixed into the hulled grains, making it difficult to separate. (3) In addition to the foot pedal, which can be used to apply force slightly due to the lever effect, the rotation of the cylinder has not been applied with any force-borrowing objects, and it is even more inconvenient to have two people work together and step on it at the same time.

▲ Overview of Improvement Methods

According to the above-mentioned shortcomings, it can be improved as follows:

(1) Add a 35 kg flywheel to the left end of the cylinder. Sensen iron can be used. The diameter should be 1 meter. The thickness of the edge can be differentiated according to the material. Then, due to inertia, it can help rotate and save a lot of effort.

(2) Install a fox-faced shield board in front of the cylinder to prevent the grains from scattering and returning to the container.

(3) Since the flywheel has been added, the power of one person can maintain it, and there is no need for two people to step on it at the same time. Therefore, the length of the machine box can be narrowed, and 60 cm is enough.

(4) Two fan-shaped leaf blades with a length of 40 cm are installed in the flywheel inner file to make them rotate smoothly, blowing the short rice straw out of the box to replace the winnowing.

(5) If the fuselage is too short after adding the flywheel leaves and wooden boards, it may be placed on a wooden box container underneath, the volume of which is 60 cm high, 60 cm wide, and 90 cm long; which is equal to the improved machine box volume; then, when the machine parts are not in use, the blades, shield wooden boards, foot pedals, etc. can be stored in the storage, and like two and a half tables, they can be picked up and transported, and when in use, they can sleep horizontally on the ground to hold grains, one move is used several times, although it costs more, but its use is infinite. And if you unload the flywheel and mention the three grains of heart that are needed for promoting national goods Xie Dihuan writes

If the two boxes are combined, in an economical family, adding a tabletop can be used as a dining table, which is even more convenient and practical.

The above is only the reporter's humble opinion. I hope that people with knowledge will make corrections, and I hope that the local gentry of each township will invest in manufacturing, and must seek more shipments, and do not have to calculate the thickness of the interest, so as to revitalize the rural economy. The reporter hopes.
